<script>
    var isPageIdle = true;
    $(document).click(function()
    {
        isPageIdle = false;
    });

    offerHotelCrossSell();

    function offerHotelCrossSell ()
    {
        var tripData = getPendingTrip ();
        if (tripData != "")
        {
            var dest = tripData.substring (12,  15);
            var o    = tripData.substring (15,  25);
            var d    = tripData.substring (25,  35);
            getHotelOffer (dest, o, d);
        }
    }

    function getPendingTrip ()
    {
        var tripData = "";
        var v        = document.cookie;
        var ndx      = v.indexOf("pendingTrip=");
        if (ndx != -1)
        {
            tripData = v.substring(ndx);
        }
        return tripData;
    }

	function getHotelOffer (destAirport, checkInDate, checkOutDate)
	{
        var path = "/flight/getHotelsExistingTrip.json" +
                   "?marketSearchKeyword=" + destAirport +
                   "&checkInDate=07%2F14%2F2011" +
                   "&checkOutDate=07%2F16%2F2011";

        var ajaxConf =
        {
            timeout:  60000,
            url:      "/flight/getHotelsExistingTrip.json?marketSearchKeyword=" + destAirport + "&checkInDate=" + encodeURIComponent(checkInDate) + "&checkOutDate=" + encodeURIComponent(checkOutDate),
            dataType: "text",
            success:  updateCallback
        };
        $.ajax(ajaxConf);

        function updateCallback (data, textStatus, xhr)
        {
            if (isPageIdle)
            {
                if (textStatus == "success")
                {
                    data = JSON.parse(data);
                    var name  = data.name;
                    var price = data.price;
                    var thumb = data.thumb;
                }

                $("#offer-heading")     .html("Book <span style='font-weight:bold; font-size:16px'>" + name + "</span> for your trip to <strong>" + getDestAirport(destAirport) + "</strong>! Rooms from under <span style='color:green; font-weight:bold'>$" + Math.ceil(price) + "</span>!");
                $("#offer-details-img") .attr("src", thumb);
                $("#offer-date-details").html("Your Travel Dates:<br/><strong>" + getMonth(checkInDate) + " " + getDay(checkInDate) + " - " + getMonth(checkOutDate) + " " + getDay(checkOutDate) + "</strong>");

                var left = $("#sw_content").offset().left + 450;
                $("#offer-details-container").css({left:left}).fadeIn("slow");
            }
        }

        function getDestAirport(destAirport)
        {
            destAirport = destAirport.toLowerCase();
            if (destAirport == "aus")
            {
                return "Austin";
            }
            if ((destAirport == "lga") || (destAirport == "isp"))
            {
                return "New York";
            }
            if (destAirport == "mdw")
            {
                return "Chicago";
            }
        }

        function getMonth(date)
        {
            var mons = ["", "Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun", "Jul", "Aug", "Sep", "Oct", "Nov", "Dec"];
            return mons[parseInt(date.substring(0, 2), 10)];
        }

        function getDay(date)
        {
            return date.substring(3, 5);
        }

	}

    function closeOffer()
    {
        $("#offer-details-container").css({display:"none"});
    }
</script>

<div id="offer-details-container" style="position:absolute; top:190px; left:200px; width:270px; height:250px; font-size:15px; z-index:1000; background:url(/assets/images/offer-background.gif); display:none">
    <div id="close-offer" style="float:right; margin-right:15px; margin-top:6px; font-size:11px">
        <a href="javascript:closeOffer()" style="float:left; margin-top:2px; margin-right:4px">close</a>
        <a href="javascript:closeOffer()" style="float:left"><img src="/assets/images/close_button.gif" border="0"/></a>
    </div>
    <div id="offer-heading" style="float:left; margin-left:15px; width:240px; line-height:20px; height:85px">
    </div>
    <a href='/hotels/search-hotels.html' style='float:left; margin-left:15px; margin-top:2px; font-size:14px'>See other hotel offers...</a>
